<h1>Pokémon item list</h1>
<div class="panel panel-intro">
<p>This is a full list of <em>every Pokémon item</em> from all 9 generations of the game series. Items from the Key pocket of the bag (such as the Bike or Super Rod) are listed on the separate <a href="/item/type/key">key items page</a>.</p>
<p>Click an item name to see even more detailed information.
		You can click a column heading to instantly sort by that column, or type in the box to filter the items.</p>
</div>

<input class="input-text" data-filter-col="0,1,2" id="filter-item-name" type="text"/>

<select data-filter-col="1" data-filter-hash="cat" id="filter-item-cat">
<option value="">- All -</option>

<option value="machines">Machines</option>
<option value="medicine">Medicine</option>
<option value="pokeballs">Pokeballs</option>
<option value="unknown">Unknown</option>
</select>
</div>
